     <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
      Top 100 Melee Players of All Time
     </h1>
     <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
      <div id="siteSub">
       From SmashWiki, the Super Smash Bros. wiki
      </div>
      <div dir="ltr" id="contentSub" lang="en">
      </div>
      <div id="jump-to-nav">
      </div>

       Jump to navigation
      </a>
      <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">
       Jump to search
      </a>
      <!-- start content -->
      <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
       <div id="adBannerTop" style="min-height:90px; text-align:center; margin:-10px 0 10px; z-index:4">

       <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="table-layout:fixed;direction:rtl" width="100%">
        <tr style="direction:ltr">
         <td id="adTower" valign="top" width="166px">
          <div style="margin:0 -4px 3px 10px; z-index:5">
           <div class="ad-tag" data-ad-name="Tower2_160x600_Sticky" data-ad-refresh="time 30s" data-ad-size="160x600" data-ad-sticky="sidebar">

         <td style="overflow:hidden" valign="top">
          <div class="mw-parser-output">
           <div>
           </div>
           <p>
            The
            <b>
             Top 100 Melee Players of All Time
            </b>
            is a project by Smash History creators
            <a class="new" href="/Smasher:Edwin_Budding?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Smasher:Edwin Budding (page does not exist)">
             Edwin Budding
            </a>
            and
            <a class="new" href="/Smasher:Pikachu942?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Smasher:Pikachu942 (page does not exist)">
             Pikachu942
            </a>
            that subjectively ranks the most successful
            <i>
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/Melee" title="Melee">
              Melee
             </a>
            </i>
            players from the middle of 2004 to the beginning of 2018, up to
            <a href="/Tournament:GENESIS_5" title="Tournament:GENESIS 5">
             GENESIS 5
            </a>
            . Since the release of the original list, Pikachu942 has made yearly updates to the Top 50.
           </p>
           <div aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading" class="toc" id="toc" role="navigation">
            <input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/>
            <div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="en">

           </div>
           <h2>
            <span class="mw-headline" id="The_Melee_Stats_All-Time_Top_100">
             The Melee Stats All-Time Top 100
            </span>
            <span class="mw-editsection">
             <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
              [
             </span>
             <a href="/Top_100_Melee_Players_of_All_Time?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: The Melee Stats All-Time Top 100">
              edit
             </a>
             <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
              ]
             </span>
            </span>
           </h2>
           <p>
            The list, made in conjunction with
            <a class="mw-disambig" href="/Panda" title="Panda">
             PGStats
            </a>
            , had several changes, including several other factors for consideration as well as a larger panel. The list was released in increments, starting with 91-100 on November 1st, 2021, and ending with 1-10 on November 21st. An "honorable exclusions" list was released in the methodology and featured players who weren't considered due to the difficulty of comparing them to the rest of the scene.
           </p>

           <h2>
            <span class="mw-headline" id="All-Time_Melee_Top_100:_Another_Year">
             All-Time Melee Top 100: Another Year
            </span>
            <span class="mw-editsection">
             <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
              [
             </span>
             <a href="/Top_100_Melee_Players_of_All_Time?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: All-Time Melee Top 100: Another Year">
              edit
             </a>
             <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
              ]
             </span>
            </span>
           </h2>
           <p>

            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/Smash_Summit_9" title="Smash Summit 9">
             Smash Summit 9
            </a>
            .

           <h2>
            <span class="mw-headline" id="All-Time_Melee_Top_100:_One_Year_Later">
             All-Time Melee Top 100: One Year Later
            </span>
            <span class="mw-editsection">
             <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
              [
             </span>
             <a href="/Top_100_Melee_Players_of_All_Time?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: All-Time Melee Top 100: One Year Later">
              edit
             </a>
             <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
              ]
             </span>
